(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

            Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

            Hint: 
            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.
            2. If you want to slice an object, you should first go to the receptacle where both the sharp object and the aim object are located and ONLY pick up the sharp object then do the slice action. Don't forget to put the sharp object back to the receptacle after you finish slicing.
            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.
        
        Note: 
        1. some receptacles have numbers in their names. Always keep them as they are. For example, "towelholder1" should not be changed to "towelholder".
        2. Your initial goal should always be to go to a new location instead of put something into somewhere.
        3. Do not enter stage 2 when not finishing stage 1.

        Note: Always include :negative-preconditions in your :requirements whenever you use (not …) or delete effects, and never leave an :precondition or :effect block empty—either omit it or include at least one literal.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)

                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)

                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

Generated df and pf:
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

            Goal 1.1: Reach a location that has not been visited (the location should be a receptacle) using the GotoLocation action. 
                You goal should look like this:
                (:goal 
                    (at ?recepatacle)
                ) where recepatacle should be somewhere or some recepatacles not visited.

                (:goal

            This may involve more than simply transferring it from one place to another.
            For example: You might examine the object or a nearby receptacle to gather information. You may need to use another tool or device (like a lamp or a switch). Some tasks require you to slice, heat, cool, or clean the object using an appropriate receptacle (e.g., microwave, sink, fridge).

            If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
            Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

            Hint: 
            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (currentAt ?r - receptacle)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?o - object)
    (holdsAny)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (currentAt ?from)
    :effect (and
                (not (currentAt ?from))
                (currentAt ?to)
                (visited ?to)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (not (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (openable ?r)
                    (opened ?r)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (pickupable ?o)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                    (not (holdsAny))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (holds ?o)
                (holdsAny)
                (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (holds ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (exists (?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
                        (and
                            (objectType ?o ?ot)
                            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
                            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
                        )
                    )
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (holds ?o))
                (not (holdsAny))
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
)

(:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (toggleable ?o)
                    (exists (?r - receptacle)
                        (and
                            (currentAt ?r)
                            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                        )
                    )
                  )
    :effect (and
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (heatable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (cleanable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isClean ?o)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (coolable ?o)
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
                    (holds ?o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)

(:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and
                    (currentAt ?r)
                    (inReceptacle ?co ?r)
                    (objectType ?sharp_o SharpObjectType)
                    (sliceable ?co)
                    (holds ?sharp_o)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (isSliced ?co)
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
            )
)
)
